============================================================
GT Equivalence Verification (CRK33)
============================================================
GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A**c2 + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))
Candidate formulas: 50

GT is the fixed function (in variables \(t,A\)):
\[
f(t,A)= -0.11846873325639269\,A^{1/2}\;-\;0.11846873325639269\,A^{2}\;+\;0.84638280991099803\,\sin(\log(A+1)).
\]
Key structural facts:
- **No \(t\)-dependence at all** (the \(t\) factor has already been absorbed into the numeric coefficient; the GT numeric expression depends only on \(A\)).
- It contains **three distinct \(A\)-dependencies**: \(A^{1/2}\), \(A^2\), and \(\sin(\log(A+1))\).
- Any candidate must be able (by parameter choice) to produce exactly these terms and no others, for all \(A,t\).

Now check candidates:

1. \(A\) linear terms + \(A^{c2}\exp(c4 t)\) + constants + \(t\exp(c7 t)\). Cannot create \(A^{1/2}\) or \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). Also has unavoidable \(t\)-structure unless coefficients set to 0, but then still lacks sine/log. **No**.

2. Polynomial/power sum \(c0A^2+c1A+c3A^{c2}+c4\). No \(\sqrt A\) unless \(c2=1/2\), but still no \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). **No**.

3. Rational combination of algebraic powers over \((A c1+1)\) plus \(c9 A^{c8}\). No way to generate \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). **No**.

4. Algebraic powers + \(\tanh(\cdot)\) in \(t\). To match GT (no \(t\)), must set tanh term to constant or zero; still no \(\sin(\log(A+1))\). **No**.

5. Similar: algebraic + \(\exp(c4 t)\), tanh, and \((|A|+1)^{c9}\). No sine/log. **No**.

6. Algebraic/rational + constant. No sine/log. **No**.

7. Algebraic + tanh + \(\exp(c7 t)\). No sine/log; also \(t\)-dependence unless killed. **No**.

8. Algebraic/rational + linear \(A\). No sine/log. **No**.

9. Algebraic + tanh + \(e^{c8 t}/A^5\). No sine/log. **No**.

10. Algebraic + tanh + constant. No sine/log. **No**.

11. \(A\) linear + \(1/(c2+t)\) + \(\exp(c5\sin(Ac6+c7))\). Has sine but of **linear \(A\)** inside, and inside an exponential; GT needs \(\sin(\log(A+1))\) additively. Cannot transform to that for all \(A\). **No**.

12. Algebraic + \(A^{c2}\exp(c4 t)\) + tanh. No sine/log. **No**.

13. Linear \(A\) + rational term \(A^{c2}/(A^{c2}+c4)\) + \(e^{c7 t}/A^5\). No sine/log. **No**.

14. tanh in \(t\) + saturating rational in \(A\). No sine/log. **No**.

15. Algebraic + tanh + \(\exp(A^{c7}c8)\). No sine/log. **No**.

16. \(A^{c0}c1 + t e^{c3 t} + e^{c5 e^{c6 t}}\). No sine/log; also \(t\)-dependence. **No**.

GT: -c0*sqrt(A) - c1*A**c2 + c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))

I need to compare each candidate against the Ground Truth (GT):

**GT:** `-0.11847*sqrt(A) - 0.11847*A^2 + 0.84638*sin(log(A + 1))`

Note: The GT has `_t = 7.144356...` which is a fixed constant, so `c3*_t*sin(log(A + c4))` becomes `0.84638*sin(log(A+1))`. The GT is actually a function of A only (t is absorbed into the constant).

Key basis functions in GT:
1. `sqrt(A)` — i.e., `A^(1/2)`
2. `A^2`
3. `sin(log(A + 1))`

This is a very specific combination. Let me check each candidate.

**Candidate 1:** `A*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3*exp(c4*t) + c5 + c6*t*exp(c7*t)`
This has terms: linear in A, `A^c2*exp(c4*t)`, constant, `t*exp(c7*t)`. The `t*exp(c7*t)` term cannot be zeroed unless c6=0, and `exp(c4*t)` can be made constant. But there's no `sin(log(A+1))` term. With `A^c2` we could get `sqrt(A)` or `A^2` but not both, and we'd still need `sin(log(...))`.
Candidate 1 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 2:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A^c2*c3 + c4`

Candidate 2 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 3:** Rational functions of A with various fractional powers. No `sin(log(...))` term. Cannot match.
Candidate 3 verdict: [NO MATCH]

**Candidate 4:** `A^2*c0 + A*c1 + A*c2 + A^c3*c4 + c5*tanh(c6*t + c7)`
Has `A^2`, `A`, `A^c3`, `tanh(c6*t+c7)`. The `tanh` is a constant (since t is a variable, but wait — is t a variable or fixed?). 

Wait, I need to reconsider. The GT has `_t` as a fixed constant (7.144...), but `t` appears as a feature variable. Let me re-read: "Feature variables: t, A". So t IS a variable. But in the GT numerical expression, `_t` has been substituted as 7.144..., making the GT independent of t.

So the GT is actually independent of t. Any candidate with t-dependence must have those t-dependent terms zeroed out.

**Candidate 4:** Setting c5=0 eliminates tanh. Left with `A^2*c0 + A*(c1+c2) + A^c3*c4`. This gives `A^2 + A + A^c3`. Setting c3=0.5 gives sqrt(A), but still has linear A term and no `sin(log(A+1))`.

Candidate 5 verdict: [NO MATCH]
